(The character of Cassard is continued from Demy''s earlier film _Lola (1961)_ (qv).) Guy is wounded and is discharged before his two-year term is up, but when he returns to Cherbourg GeneviÃ¨ve has already married and moved away. He struggles with depression and anger, but eventually is healed by falling in love with and marrying Madeleine, a young woman who had been caring for his now-deceased aunt Ãlise. Using an inheritance from his aunt, Guy fulfills his ambition of opening a service station. Years later, the now conspicuously wealthy GeneviÃ¨ve, traveling with her daughter, Guy''s child, accidentally meet Guy at his service station.
